 issebhi partiyon ko ek maukamilegaa

 iske alaava court ne yah bhi kaha ki pehle bhi desh main alpamat kii sarkarein bani hai

 notebandi kaa asar ab gaanv kii arthvyavastha par dikhne laga he
 The economy of agriculture running on the strength of cash is peaking due to not having cash
 ek taraf kisaan pareshaan he duusari ore bunakar
 The situation is worse for those who do not have their own accounts and those who were merely making a living with cash
 un kisaanon ko jinhen is vakt apane kheton main buvaai ke liye hona chahie tha wo is vakt bainkon ke chakkar laga rahe hai

 ek taraf nagdi kaa sankat duusari ore chote kasbon main sahakaari bainkon se note badalane or jamaa karne par lagi roak se kisaanon kii pareshaani bad gai he

 Let us know some special things about Ashok Kumar Saheb
 1
 Ashok Kumar was born on 13 October 1911 in Bhagalpur Bihar
 2
 At the time of his birth, he was named 'kumudlal Ganguly' and in the film industry he was affectionately called 'dadamuni (elder brother)'
 3
 Ashok Kumar's father Kunjlal Ganguly was a lawyer and his mother was a domestic woman
 ashok ghar ke bade ladke the unke baad unki bahan sati devi phir bhai kishor kumaar or anup kumaar the
 4
 ashok kumaar kaa bachapan se hi film industry main kaam karne kaa sapana tha lekin actor ke rup main nahin balki technitian ke rup main
 5
 un dinon ashok kumaar ke bahanoi sashadhar mukherjee mumbai main 'bombai tokies' main oonche pad par kaam kiya karte the, jisaki vajah seashok kumaar mumbai aa gaeor bombai tokies main hi 'lab assistant' ke rup main kaam karne lage
 6
 saal 1936 kii bombai tokies ke antargat ban rahi film 'jivan naiya' kii shooting shuru hone se pehle hi uske lead actors devika rani or najmul hasan ke bich matbhed ho gaye, jisaki vajah se film ke produsar himanshu raay ne najmul kii jagah kumudlal (ashok kumaar) ko film main bulaayaa haalanki film ke diarector is baat se naakhush the, lekin phir bhi himanshu ne unhen film main liya or pehali baar kumudlal ganguli kaa screen naam 'ashok kumaar' rakh diya gaya kyonki un dinon actors apane asli naam ko parde par nahin ujagar karte the
 7
